By the time the final quarter arrived, Collins got a sense of familiarity watching his teammate.,I know what time it is. Its Ice Trae time. Hes clutch. He wants to be in that moment. I mean, they arent doing that to everybody, he said.,Boston pushed the ball up the court and got the ball to Robert Williams, who dropped in a layup. Young hit all three free throws to put the Hawks in front 114-113.,Brown turned it over, then misfired on a driving layup. Atlantas next possession ended in a jump ball that was controlled by Boston.
